                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">شَآمِيَّةٌ تَسْتَجْمِعُ الشَّوْلَ حَرْجَفُ</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> [<hi rend="ital">A north wind, cold and vehement, inviting to collect themselves together the she-camels whose milk has dried up, they having passed seven or eight months since bringing forth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">since pregnancy</hi>], it seems that he has compared this verb with the generality of others of the same class, [and so derived the meaning in which he has here used it,] or that he heard it [in that sense] from the people of the cities, or towns, or villages, and cultivated lands.                   </form> and <foreign lang="ar">مَجْمِعٌ</foreign>, (S, Msb, K,) the latter anomalous, like <foreign lang="ar">مَشْرِقٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَغْرِبٌ</foreign> &amp;c., (TA,) <hi rend="ital">A place of collecting, and the like:</hi> (S, Msb, * K:) [pl. <foreign lang="ar">مَجَامِعُ</foreign>] [Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">مَجْمَعُ البَحْرَيْنِ</foreign>, in the Kur [xviii. 59], means <hi rend="ital">The place where the two seas meet.</hi> (Bd.)                   <foreign lang="ar">وَكَتِفِى</foreign>, [in which <foreign lang="ar">مَا</foreign> seems to have been dropped by the copyist between <foreign lang="ar">مجمع</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بين</foreign>,] the meaning is, [<hi rend="ital">And he struck with his hand</hi>] <hi rend="ital">the place where my neck and my shoulder-blade meet.</hi> (TA.) [Hence also the phrase <foreign lang="ar">مَجَامِعُ المَحَامِدِ</foreign>, explained above: see <foreign lang="ar">جَامِعٌ</foreign>, near the end of the paragraph. And <foreign lang="ar">مَجَامِعُ الأُمُورِ</foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">The concurrences of affairs,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of circumstances,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of events.</hi>]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A place in which people collect, assemble,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">congregate:</hi> (Msb, * TA:) and [in like manner,]   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6326-1" target="مَجْمَعَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6330"/></foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">an assembly-room; a sitting room in which people assemble:</hi> (TA:) [pl. of both <foreign lang="ar">مَجَامِعُ</foreign>.] You say, <foreign lang="ar">هٰذَا الكَلَامُ أَوْلَجُ فِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">المَسَامِعِ وَأَجْوَلُ فِى المَجَامِعِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">This language,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">discourse, is more,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">most, penetrating into the ears, and more,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">most, circulating in the places of assembly</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">جَمْعٌ</foreign>, as syn. with <foreign lang="ar">جَمَاعَةٌ</foreign>, in two places; and see 10, first sentence.          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  [The <hi rend="ital">whole</hi> of anything, considered as the place in which the several parts thereof are collected: see an instance voce <foreign lang="ar">خُفٌّ</foreign>: and see also <foreign lang="ar">مُجْتَمَعٌ</foreign>.]    </entryFree>34:T672,<entryFree id="n6333" key="مُجْتَمَعٌ" type="main">

                  <hi rend="ital">A year of dearth, drought, sterility,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">unfruitfulness:</hi> (Ks, K:) because it is an occasion of people's collecting together in the place where herbage, or plenty, is found. (Ks.) And <foreign lang="ar">فَلَاةٌ مُجْمِعَةٌ</foreign>, (S, TA,) like <foreign lang="ar">مُحْسِنَةٌ</foreign>; (TA;) [in Gol. Lex., erroneously, <foreign lang="ar">مُجْمَعَةٌ</foreign>;] and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6328-1" target="مُجَمِّعَةٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, like <foreign lang="ar">مُحَدِّثَةٌ</foreign>; (TA;) <hi rend="ital">A desert in which people collect themselves together, not separating themselves, from fear of losing their way, or perishing, and the like;</hi> as though the desert itself collected them. (S, TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">أَرْضٌ مُجْمِعَةٌ</foreign>, like <foreign lang="ar">مُحْسِنَةٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">A land of dearth, drought, sterility,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">unfruitfulness, wherein the camels upon which people journey are not dispersed to pasture.</hi> (TA.)    </entryFree>36:T538,<entryFree id="n6334" key="مُجْتَمِعٌ" type="main">
